<script type="text/javascript">
	
	 var directionVal;
	 var textpositionDesktop = "left";
	 var textpositionMobile = "left";
	 var textposition = textpositionDesktop;
	 var C1HeroImageTeadDropNode = "heroimage_teardrop_s";
	 var parentElement = '.heroimage-teardrop-desktop';
	 if(($(window).width() <= 750) && $('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').length){
		parentElement = '.heroimage-teardrop-mobile';
		textposition = textpositionMobile;
	 }
	 if(C1HeroImageTeadDropNode==""){
	 	 C1HeroImageTeadDropNode = "imagery1";
	 }
	 var $C1TearDropHeaderImage = $(parentElement+' .'+C1HeroImageTeadDropNode);
	 var $C1TearDropMobileImageURL = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('mobile-image');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImageURL = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('desktop-image');
	 var $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-mobile-fadeColor');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-desktop-fadeColor');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg =  $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('bg');
	 var $mobileImagedataBg = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('mobile-bg');
	 var $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop  = true;
	 var $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = true;
	 var directionType = $('#fadeValue').val();
	if(directionType == "qr.arabic"){
         if(textposition == "left" || textposition == "center") {
   		 	directionVal =  "to left";
         }
         else {
			directionVal =  "to right";
         }
     } 
     else {

         if(textposition == "left" || textposition == "center") {
   		 	directionVal =  "to right";
         }
         else {
			directionVal =  "to left";
         }
     }

    $(document).ready(function() {

    imageLoad();

    });

	$(window).on('load',function(){
    imageLoad();

    });


function imageLoad() {


        if($C1TearDropMobileImageURL =='url();'){

        $C1TearDropMobileImageURL=$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL;
        $mobileImagedataBg = $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg;
        $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor =$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor;

   		}

		if($(window).width() <= 750){
			if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile)
			{
				if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
		   		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
		   		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		  		}else{
		  	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
		 	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL);
                    $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		  		}

				$C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = false;
			}else
			{
				if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
               		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
		  		}else{
		  	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'");');
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		  		}


           	}

        }else {
         	if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop)
			{
				if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL+'background-size: cover');
				}else{
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL);
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
				}

				$C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop= false;
			}else
           	{
				if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
				}else{
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'");');
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
				}


			 }

        }
        $(window).on('resize', function(){
			if($(this).width() <= 750){

				if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile)
				{
					if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){

                        $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");

                        $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");

				if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop)
				{
					if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);

                         $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){

	if($(window).width() <= 750){
		if($('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').length){
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').removeAttr('hidden');
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-desktop').remove();
		} else {
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-desktop').removeAttr('hidden');
		}
	} else {
		$('.heroimage-teardrop-desktop').removeAttr('hidden');
		$('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').remove();
	}
});
</script>

   <script>
       $(document).ready(function(){
      var $nodeName = "#table-module-21XQB-table_copy .C6_1";
      var tableHeaders = [];

      $($nodeName).find('table').removeAttr("cellspacing cellpadding border width");
	  $($nodeName).find('table th').each(function(){
      	tableHeaders.push($(this).text());
      });

	  if ($(window).width() < 767) {
			$($nodeName).find('table tr').each(function(i){
				var $this = $(this);
				$(this).find('td').each(function(index){
					if($(this).attr('rowspan') != undefined){
						$($nodeName).find('table tr').eq(i+1).find('td').eq(index).before('<td>'+$(this).text()+'</td>');
					}
				});
			});
        	$($nodeName).find('th').parent().hide();
      }

	var $tableRows = $($nodeName).find('tr');
      $tableRows.each(function(){
          var t = 0;
          var $tableData = $(this).find('td');
          if($tableData != undefined && $tableData != '') {
      		$tableData.each(function(){
              if(tableHeaders[t] == '&nbsp;'){

              $(this).attr("data-th",'');
              }else {
                $(this).attr("data-th", tableHeaders[t]);
              }
			  if($(window).width() < 767){
					($(this).attr('data-th') != undefined && $(this).attr('data-th').length > 45) ? $(this).css('margin-bottom',($(this).attr('data-th').length/2)+20+'px') : $(this).css('margin-bottom','0');
				}

      		t++;
      
      });
          }

      });
      $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').css('text-align','');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('width');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('valign');
});
   </script>


      </div>
   


</div>


                                           </div>
                                 </div>
                              </li>

                    <div>Your baggage allowance depends on the flight and booking class.&nbsp; You can find the number of pieces and weight allowed for your journey when you select your flights, as well as on your ticket prior to travel.<br>

<div>For routes where the baggage allowance is displayed by weight (flying from/to destinations other than Africa &amp; the Americas), there is no limit on the number of pieces that can be checked in as long as the weight allowance for the total number of pieces is not exceeded. However, limitations may apply based on aircraft carrying capacity.&nbsp;<br>

<div><b>Maximum dimensions (length + width + height)</b></div>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>When flying to/from Africa or the Americas, the maximum dimension per bag should not exceed 158cm.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>When flying from Dammam, the maximum dimension per bag must not exceed 158cm.<br>
</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>When flying from Dublin, items carried as checked baggage must not exceed 240cm as the maximum length per bag.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>When flying to/from other destinations:&nbsp;the maximum dimension per bag should not exceed 300cm.</li>
</ul>
<p><b style="background-color: transparent;">Maximum weight</b><br>
</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>A single piece of checked baggage should weigh no more than 32kg (70lb).</li>
</ul>
<p>Note: Pieces of baggage that are round, irregular-shaped, tied with loose rope or string, wrapped in blankets or that have loose straps will not be accepted.</p>

                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p>In addition to the regular checked-in baggage allowance, you may also bring along hand baggage on board the cabin during your Qatar Airways flight:</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>First Class and Business Class passengers can carry two pieces of baggage on board, not to exceed a total weight of 15kg (33lb).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Economy Class passengers can carry one piece of baggage, not to exceed 7kg (15lb).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>For tickets issued in Brazil, Economy Class customers on flights to or from Brazil can carry one piece of baggage, not to exceed 10 kg (22lb).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Maximum dimensions for each piece of hand baggage are 50x37x25cm (20x15x10in).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Laptops and laptop bags should fit within your hand baggage allowance.</li>
</ul>
<p>You can also carry personal items such as one lady’s handbag or one small briefcase; one coat, cape or blanket; one umbrella; one pair of crutches or a walking stick; one small camera or binoculars; limited reading material; an infant’s carrying basket; duty-free items purchased on the day of your flight.</p>

<p><b>Liquids and gels in hand baggage</b></p>
<p>You may carry liquids, gels, pastes and aerosols in containers up to 100ml (3.4oz) in your hand baggage. Containers larger than 100ml cannot be accepted even if only partly filled. Your containers should be carried in a transparent, resealable, quart- or litre-sized bag no larger than 20x20cm (8x8in). Please ensure all items fit comfortably in the plastic bag.</p>
<p>Airport security will ask you to produce your transparent bag of liquids separately for screening. There are no restrictions on baby foods and medication. However, you may be required to present a prescription for medication you want to take on board.</p>

<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>You may be asked by security staff to turn on personal electronic devices that are larger than a mobile phone, including tablets, e-books and laptops during the security screening conducted at the boarding gate.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Ensure your electronic device(s) has sufficient power to be switched on to demonstrate its functionality. </li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Devices without any power will be placed in a secure location on the aircraft that cannot be accessed, and returned at the final destination.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If more than six personal electronic individual devices are already secured, then you will have to check-in your device into your hand baggage, which will be stored in the aircraft hold.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If you are unable to check-in your hand baggage with the device or do not have a hand baggage, then your item will need to be deposited with <a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/lost-and-found.html" target="_self">Lost and Found</a>. You will then be required to make a claim on the airline website and collect the item from the airport on your return.&nbsp;</li>
</ul>
<p><b>USA-bound flights</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>All personal electronic devices carried on board all USA-bound flights from Doha, are subject to enhanced security screening.<br>

</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Consider packing all personal electronic devices that you do not intend to use in-flight into your check-in baggage.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Examples of personal electronic devices that are subject to enhanced security screening include: DSLR camera | Radio | E-reader | Walkie-talkie | Laptop | Tablet | Water purifier | Large game console | Monitor| CD-ROM | Drone | Electric guitar | Printer and scanner</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Additional security measures for international flights to or from the USA</b></p>

<script type="text/javascript">
	
	 var directionVal;
	 var textpositionDesktop = "left";
	 var textpositionMobile = "left";
	 var textposition = textpositionDesktop;
	 var C1HeroImageTeadDropNode = "heroimage_teardrop_s";
	 var parentElement = '.heroimage-teardrop-desktop';
	 if(($(window).width() <= 750) && $('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').length){
		parentElement = '.heroimage-teardrop-mobile';
		textposition = textpositionMobile;
	 }
	 if(C1HeroImageTeadDropNode==""){
	 	 C1HeroImageTeadDropNode = "imagery1";
	 }
	 var $C1TearDropHeaderImage = $(parentElement+' .'+C1HeroImageTeadDropNode);
	 var $C1TearDropMobileImageURL = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('mobile-image');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImageURL = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('desktop-image');
	 var $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-mobile-fadeColor');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-desktop-fadeColor');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg =  $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('bg');
	 var $mobileImagedataBg = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('mobile-bg');
	 var $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop  = true;
	 var $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = true;
	 var directionType = $('#fadeValue').val();
	if(directionType == "qr.arabic"){
         if(textposition == "left" || textposition == "center") {
   		 	directionVal =  "to left";
         }
         else {
			directionVal =  "to right";
         }
     } 
     else {

         if(textposition == "left" || textposition == "center") {
   		 	directionVal =  "to right";
         }
         else {
			directionVal =  "to left";
         }
     }

    $(document).ready(function() {

    imageLoad();

    });

	$(window).on('load',function(){
    imageLoad();

    });


function imageLoad() {


        if($C1TearDropMobileImageURL =='url();'){

        $C1TearDropMobileImageURL=$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL;
        $mobileImagedataBg = $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg;
        $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor =$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor;

   		}

		if($(window).width() <= 750){
			if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile)
			{
				if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
		   		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
		   		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		  		}else{
		  	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
		 	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL);
                    $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		  		}

				$C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = false;
			}else
			{
				if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
               		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
		  		}else{
		  	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'");');
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		  		}


           	}

        }else {
         	if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop)
			{
				if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL+'background-size: cover');
				}else{
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL);
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
				}

				$C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop= false;
			}else
           	{
				if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
				}else{
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'");');
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
				}


			 }

        }
        $(window).on('resize', function(){
			if($(this).width() <= 750){

				if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile)
				{
					if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
					}else{
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL);
                        $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
					}

					$C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = false;
				}else
				{
					if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
					}else{
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'");');
                        $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
					}


				}
			}else {

				if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop)
				{
					if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL+'background-size: cover');
					}else{
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL);
                         $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
					}

					$C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop= false;
				}else
				{
					if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');

        });

     };

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){

	if($(window).width() <= 750){
		if($('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').length){
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').removeAttr('hidden');
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-desktop').remove();
		} else {
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-desktop').removeAttr('hidden');
		}
	} else {
		$('.heroimage-teardrop-desktop').removeAttr('hidden');
		$('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').remove();
	}
});
</script>

     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Passengers may carry ammunition in their checked baggage on a Qatar Airways flight if it is declared to the airline at check in. The required licences and documentation for their ammunition must be provided to the appropriate local authorities in the States they are flying to and from.</p>
<p>Only ammunition classified as UN0012 and UN0014 are allowed in passenger baggage, in quantities not exceeding a gross weight of 5 kg per person.</p>
<p>Note:&nbsp; What is a UN number?&nbsp; It is a four-digit number assigned by the United Nations Committee of Experts (UNCOE) on the Transport of Dangerous Goods, identifying a substance or a particular group of substances or articles. The “Safety data sheet” (SDS) of the ammunition will provide this information, generally under the Section 14 of the SDS.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Ammunition shall be packed separately from the baggage containing the firearm, inside a robust, secure container (i.e., a strong wooden, metal or fiberboard box or other packaging) specially designed to carry small amounts of ammunition and capable of being locked.</p>
<p>Ammunition may only be carried for individual use. Ammunition for use by more than one passenger may not be combined into one or more packages and carried by one passenger in the booking.&nbsp;</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Firearms</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Passengers may carry one or more firearms in their checked baggage on a Qatar Airways flight if they are declared to the airline at check in. A ‘Declaration of Surrender of Firearms’ must be signed and the required licences and documentation for their firearms, must be provided to the appropriate local authorities in the States they are flying to and from.</p>
<p>Firearms must be unloaded and packaged appropriately in a hard-side, lockable container. The baggage containing the firearms must be locked before being accepted for carriage.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>



        </div>
</div>




                                
                                
                                
                                    

	
<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Batteriesandbatterypowereddevices">
    <h3>Batteries and battery-powered devices</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Batteries and battery-powered devices</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Please switch off all battery-powered devices, if they are carried in your checked baggage. Do not place them in sleep or hibernation mode, and ensure that you take measures to prevent unintentional activation and damage to your device(s).&nbsp;</p>
<p>Also, please individually protect the terminals of each spare battery to prevent short circuits, through placing the batteries in their original retail packaging or insulating terminals. You may insulate terminals by&nbsp;positioning an adhesive tape over exposed terminals, or packing each battery into a separate plastic bag or protective pouch.&nbsp;Spare batteries are allowed in hand baggage only.&nbsp;If the primary purpose of any equipment is to power another equipment, then they are considered as batteries and appropriate restrictions for standalone batteries will apply. Examples for such equipment – Power banks (even when they are comprising with other small features, such as flash-light) / Jump-Starters (even when they are with in-built air-pumps and or containing flash- lights, etc.)</p>
<p>According to international regulations governing the air transportation, all types of lithium batteries (spare, in equipment, packed with equipment) must be of a type that meets the requirements of the UN Manual of Test and Criteria, Part III, subsection 38.3.&nbsp;</p>
<p><a href="#lithium">Click here for more information on lithium batteries.</a></p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Drones (Remotely-piloted aircraft system – RPAS)</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry drones with or without batteries in your hand baggage.<br>
</p>
<p>Batteries in drones and/or spare batteries, with a watt-hour (Wh) rating exceeding 100 Wh up to 160 Wh, must be approved by Qatar Airways before you may carry them in your hand baggage. You may not carry batteries in drones and/or spare batteries, with a watt-hour rating exceeding 160 Wh, in your hand or checked baggage.</p>
<p>You may carry drones without batteries in your checked baggage. The removed battery/batteries may be carried in your hand baggage, if they adhere to the regulations regarding spare batteries.&nbsp;Drone battery must not be charged during your flight.</p>
<p>Various countries have restrictions that may impact the carriage and entry of drones. Please ensure that you refer to the local rules and regulations of your destination country before travelling.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>e-Cigarettes</h4>

     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry e-Cigarettes including e-cigars, e-pipes and other personal&nbsp;vaporizers containing batteries, in your hand baggage.&nbsp;Recharging of the equipment or the battery on board the aircraft is not permitted.<br>
</p>
</div>

    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">

     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>*This item is only allowed when carried on the person</p>
<p>You may carry one e-Cigarette lighter such as a laser plasma lighter, tesla coil lighter, flux lighter, arc lighter or double arc lighter, powered by lithium batteries, with you. Please ensure that your lighter is protected by a safety cap. It must not be placed in hand or checked baggage. Recharging of the equipment or the battery on board the aircraft is not permitted.</p>
</div>

     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Portable electronic devices (PED)</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry portable electronic devices (PED), including portable medical electronic devices (PMED), in your hand and checked baggage. PED include cameras, mobile phones, laptops, tablets or any equipment&nbsp;containing batteries that provide electrical power for operation.*<br>
</p>
<p>Your device(s) may contain the following types of batteries: Typical AA, AAA, C, D, 9-volt,&nbsp;button-sized cells, rechargeable &amp; non-rechargeable lithium batteries Nickel Metal Hydride (NiMH), Nickel Cadmium (NiCad), etc.</p>
<p>If you carry PED in your checked baggage, please switch them all off. Do not place them in sleep or hibernation mode, and ensure that you take measures to prevent unintentional activation and damage to your device(s).</p>
<p>* You may carry a maximum of 15 PEDs.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p>When they are powered by lithium batteries, the watt-hour rating must not exceed 100 for lithium ion batteries and the lithium content must not exceed 2g for lithium metal batteries.&nbsp; &nbsp;</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Portable electronic devices (PED) containing lithium batteries</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry portable electronic devices (PED) containing lithium ion batteries, including portable medical electronic devices (PMED) containing lithium metal or lithium ion batteries, in your hand and checked baggage.</p>
<p>PEDs &amp; PMEDs containing lithium batteries include consumer electronics, video cameras, power tools, portable oxygen concentrators (POC), automated external defibrillators (AED), continuous positive airway pressure (CPAP) and any equipment containing lithium cells or batteries, which provide electrical power for operation.<br>
</p>
<p>Only PMED may contain lithium metal batteries with lithium content exceeding 2g up to 8g.&nbsp;<br>
</p>
<p>PED &amp; PMED may contain lithium ion batteries with a watt-hour (Wh) rating exceeding 100 Wh up to 160 Wh.</p>
<p>If you carry PED in your checked baggage, please switch them all off. Do not place them in sleep or hibernation mode, and ensure that you take measures to prevent unintentional activation and damage to your device(s).</p>
<p>Spare batteries for such devices:</p>
<p>PEDs/PMEDs – Only a total of 02 spare lithium-ion batteries are allowed.</p>
<p>PMEDs – Only a total of 02 spare lithium metal batteries are allowed.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Smart baggage</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Qatar Airways has specific restrictions in regards to the transportation of ‘smart baggage.’</p>
<p>Smart baggage devices often have:</p>
<p>- A lithium ion battery power bank that charges electronic devices such as mobile phones and laptops</p>
<p>- A lithium ion battery that is used for a stand up scooter or sit on vehicle</p>
<p>- Bluetooth, radio frequency identification and Wi-Fi capability</p>
<p>- GPS tracking with or without GSM capability</p>
<p>- Electronic baggage tags</p>
<p>- Electronic locks</p>
<p>- Self-propelled baggage</p>
<p>Smart baggage equipped with a permanently fixed (non-removable) lithium battery is not allowed as ‘carry-on’ or as ‘checked baggage.’</p>
<p>Smart baggage equipped with a removable lithium battery can only be accepted as checked baggage if the battery is removed. The removed lithium battery must then be carried on board by the passenger and must remain in their hand baggage.&nbsp;</p>
<p>If your smart baggage is brought on board as a carry-on, the lithium battery must remain in the baggage. When transporting, measures must be taken to prevent unintentional activation and to protect the device from damage. The device must be completely switched off (not in sleep or hibernation mode).</p>
<p>The rules above do not apply to smart baggage equipped only with lithium button cells.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Spare or loose batteries - All types, including small lithium batteries</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry spare or loose batteries for portable electronic devices (PED), and portable medical&nbsp;electronic devices (PMED).*</p>
<p>Each lithium metal battery may have lithium content not exceeding 2g.&nbsp;In addition, each lithium ion battery may have a watt-hour (Wh) rating not exceeding 100 Wh.</p>
<p>Other types includes –Dry batteries, Nickel Cadmium batteries, Alkaline batteries, etc.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p>*You may carry a maximum of 20 spare batteries.<br>
</p>



</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Vehicles powered by lithium batteries</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        
			<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-blocked"></span> Not allowed</div>
		

		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">

        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may not carry small vehicles powered by lithium batteries in your hand or checked baggage, even if the batteries are removed. This is applicable regardless of the watt-hour rating of the batteries. In addition, you may not carry smart vechiles.</p>
<p>Examples – Airwheels, Solowheels, Hover-boards, Mini-Segways,&nbsp;E-scooters, and Balance-wheels.&nbsp;</p>

    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Avalanche rescue backpack</h4>

        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry one avalanche rescue backpack, containing cartridges of compressed gas in Division 2.2, without a subsidiary hazard. Your backpack may also be equipped with a pyrotechnic trigger mechanism containing no more than 200mg net of Division 1.4S explosives.</p>
<p>Please pack your backpack in such a manner that it cannot be accidentally activated. The airbags within your backpack must be fitted with pressure relief valves.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>

    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">

        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry small cylinders of a non-flammable and non-toxic gas, of Division 2.2, worn for the operation of mechanical limbs, in your hand and checked baggage. You may also carry spare cylinders of a similar size if required, to ensure that you have an adequate supply of gas for the duration of your journey.&nbsp;</p>

     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Small non-flammable gas cartridges </h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry small non-flammable gas cartridges, containing carbon dioxide or another suitable gas in Division 2.2, without a subsidiary hazard, fitted into a self-inflating personal safety device (such as Life-vest).&nbsp;</p>
<p>Please ensure that:</p>
<p>- Only up to two small cartridges are fitted into a self-inflating safety device such as a life jacket or vest</p>
<p>- You carry a maximum of two safety devices per person</p>
<p>- Only a maximum of two small&nbsp;spare cartridges are packed for each lifesaving device</p>
<p>- Each of your devices is packed in such a manner that it cannot be accidentally activated</p>
<p>If you are planning to carry small non-flammable, non-toxic gas cartridges for other devices, such as CO<sub>2 </sub>bicycle tyre inflators, &nbsp;the allowance is – 04 cartridges per person and the maximum capacity of each cartridge must not exceed 28g (50mL water capacity).&nbsp; &nbsp;</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>

     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Hair curlers containing hydrocarbon gas</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>

</p>

</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Equipment with compressed gas</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Equipment such as small Refrigerators / Portable ACs / Water dispensers / Ice-cream makers / Ice makers, generally contain compressed gas for its operation.</p>
<p>Considering IATA dangerous goods regulations, following products are exempted from regulations, as long as they are not damaged.</p>
<ul>
<li>Machines containing non-flammable, non-toxic, liquefied compressed gas – Not considered as dangerous goods, if the amount of gas is not exceeding 12kg</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>Machines containing flammable, non-toxic, liquefied compress gas – Not considered as dangerous goods, if they are complying with following:<ul>
<li>Containing less than 100g of flammable, non-toxic, liquefied gas.</li>
<li>Machine components must be designed &amp; tested to at least three times the working pressure of the machine.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Designed &amp; constructed to contain the gas and prevent the risk of bursting or cracking of the pressure retaining components during normal condition of air-transport.&nbsp;</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>



        </div>
</div>




                                
                                
                                
                                    

	
<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Fuel">
    <h3>Fuel</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Fuel</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Camping stoves</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry a camping stove with an empty fuel tank, which has previously held a flammable liquid fuel. You may also carry an empty fuel container&nbsp;which has previously held a flammable liquid fuel.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Please ensure that:</p>
<p>- Fuel tanks of camping stoves and fuel containers are&nbsp;fully drained of all liquid fuel. To nullify danger, drain the fuel tank or container for at least one hour, then leave it uncapped for a minimum of six hours to allow any residual fuel to evaporate. Alternative methods, such as adding cooking oil to the fuel tank or container to elevate the flash point of any residual liquid, above the flash point of flammable liquid, and then emptying the fuel tank and/or container, are equally acceptable.&nbsp;</p>
<p>- Fuel tanks of camping stoves and fuel containers have a cap securely fastened.</p>
<p>- Camping stoves with an empty fuel tank and fuel containers, are wrapped in absorbent material such as paper towel, and placed in a polyethylene or equivalent bag.&nbsp;The top of the bag must then be sealed, or gathered and closed with an elastic band or twine.</p>
<p>Brand-new camping stoves or brand-new fuel containers for such camping stoves, which has never contained any flammable liquid fuel, are not considered as dangerous goods and can be carried without restrictions. However, it is advisable that you get in touch with Qatar Airways in advance, in order to get a confirmation.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Fuel cells</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry fuel cells containing fuel-powering portable electronic devices (PED) such as cameras, mobile phones, laptops and camcorders, in your hand baggage.&nbsp;</p>
<p>In addition, you may carry a maximum of two spare fuel cell cartridges&nbsp;in your hand baggage.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Additional restrictions to fuel cells apply. <a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a> for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>



        </div>

<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Liquids">
    <h3>Liquids</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Liquids</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Alcoholic Beverages </h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry alcoholic beverages in your hand and checked baggage. When in retail packaging, the beverages may contain more than 24% but not more than 70% alcohol by volume, in receptacles not exceeding 5l. The maximum&nbsp;total net quantity, of alcoholic beverages per passenger, is 5l.&nbsp;Alcoholic beverages with not more than 24% alcohol by volume, are not considered as dangerous goods by the applicable regulations.&nbsp;</p>
<p>When carried in hand baggage, the quantities may be restricted further, due to other regulations, such as LAGs.&nbsp;Please check the country/customs regulations also.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Liquids and gels</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry liquids, gels, pastes and aerosols in containers up to 100ml (3.4oz) in your hand baggage. Containers larger than 100ml cannot be accepted, even if only partly filled.</p>
<p>Your containers should be carried in a transparent, resealable, quart- or litre-sized bag no larger than 20x20cm (8x8in). Please ensure all items fit comfortably in the plastic bag.<br>
</p>
<p>Airport security will ask you to produce your transparent bag of liquids separately for screening.<br>
</p>
<p>When you are travelling with infants or have special dietary needs, you are permitted to carry reasonable quantities of food, required for the duration of the flight.&nbsp;</p>
<p>To find out more about exemptions related to carriage of baby foods, medication and special dietary requirements,&nbsp;<a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help/faq.html#liquids" target="_blank">browse our FAQs</a>.</p>

</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>



        </div>

<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Medicalitems">
    <h3>Medical items</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Medical items</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Liquid nitrogen contained in insulated packaging (Dry Shipper)</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry insulated packaging containing refrigerated liquid nitrogen (dry shipper),<b>&nbsp;</b>fully absorbed in a porous material, at a low temperature, in your hand and checked baggage.&nbsp;The packaging can contain non-dangerous items only.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Oxygen or Air cylinders for medical use</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry oxygen or air cylinders required for medical use. Each cylinder must not exceed a gross weight of 5kg.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p>You may not carry personal medical oxygen devices that utilize liquid oxygen on your person, in your hand baggage or in your checked baggage.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Radio-isotopic cardiac pacemakers</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You&nbsp;are allowed to travel with radio-isotopic cardiac pacemakers or other devices, including those powered by lithium batteries, implanted into the body or fitted externally</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Non-infectious Specimens with flammable liquids</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry non-infectious specimens packed with small quantities of flammable liquid, in your hand and checked baggage. Non-infectious specimens include specimens of mammals, birds, amphibians, reptiles, fish, insects and other invertebrates, and flammable liquids categorised under UN 1170, UN 1198, UN 1987, and UN 1219.</p>
<p>Please ensure that:</p>
<p>(a) Specimens are:&nbsp;</p>
<p>- Wrapped in paper towel and/or cheesecloth moistened with alcohol or an alcohol solution, before being placed in a plastic bag that is heat-sealed and contains free liquid not exceeding 30ml, or:</p>
<p>- Placed in vials or other rigid containers with a maximum of 30ml of alcohol or an alcohol solution;</p>
<p>(b) The prepared specimens are then placed in a plastic bag that is then heat–sealed;</p>
<p>(c) The bagged specimens are then placed inside another plastic bag made of an absorbent material and heat-sealed;&nbsp;</p>
<p>(d) The finished bag is then placed in strong outer packaging with suitable cushioning material;</p>
<p>(e) The total quantity of flammable liquid per outer packaging does not exceed 1l; and&nbsp;</p>
<p>(f) The completed package is marked, "Scientific research specimens, not restricted as per special provision A180 applies."</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Thermometer (medical or clinical)</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry one thermometer containing mercury, for your personal use, in your checked baggage. Please ensure that your thermometer is packed in a protective case.</p>
<p>You may not carry thermometers containing mercury in your hand baggage.&nbsp;</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Thermometer or barometer</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>If you are a representative of a government weather bureau or similar official agency, and you receive approval, you may carry a thermometer or barometer containing mercury, in your hand baggage.<br>
</p>
<p>The barometer or thermometer must be packed in strong outer packaging with a sealed inner liner, or a bag made of strong leak-proof and puncture-resistant material impervious to mercury, which will prevent the escape of mercury from the package, irrespective of its position.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>

<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Mobilityaids">
    <h3>Mobility aids</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Mobility aids</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Mobility aids are acceptable when the mobility of the passenger is restricted by either a disability, their health or age, or a temporary mobility problem (example – broken leg).</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Battery-powered mobility aids with non-spillable batteries</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry battery-powered wheelchairs or other similar mobility devices, with wet, non-spillable, nickel metal hydride or dry batteries. Please ensure that you take measures to prevent the unintentional activation of your mobility aid(s).</p>
<p>Non-spillable batteries may not contain any free or unabsorbed liquid. In addition, if you remove the batteries from your mobility aid(s), the removed batteries, along with any spare batteries, must be carried in strong, rigid packaging to be stored in the cargo compartment.</p>
<p>You may carry a maximum of one spare wet, non-spillable battery, or two spare nickel metal hydride or dry batteries.&nbsp;</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Battery-powered mobility aids with lithium batteries</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry battery-powered wheelchairs or other similar mobility devices, with lithium ion batteries.</p>
<p>If the battery is attached to your mobility aid, there is no limit on its watt-hour (Wh) rating.&nbsp;If you however remove the battery from your mobility aid, the battery must not exceed the watt hour rating of 300Wh. If your mobility aid is fitted with two batteries that you remove, each battery must not exceed the watt hour rating of 160Wh.</p>
<p>The removed batteries, along with any spare batteries, must be placed in a protective pouch, and be carried in the passenger cabin.&nbsp;About spare batteries - you&nbsp;may carry a maximum of one spare lithium ion battery with a Wh rating not exceeding 300 Wh,&nbsp;or a maximum of two spare lithium ion batteries, each with Wh rating not exceeding 160 Wh. Please make sure that the removed batteries are properly packed in order to prevent short-circuiting or damage.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Battery-powered mobility aids with spillable batteries</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry battery-powered wheelchairs or other similar mobility devices with spillable batteries.</p>
<p>Please ensure that the battery of your mobility aid(s) is fitted, where feasible, with spill-resistant vent caps.&nbsp;If your mobility aid cannot always be loaded, stowed, secured and unloaded in an upright position, or if your mobility aid does not adequately protect its battery, the battery must be removed.</p>
<p>The removed battery must be carried in strong, rigid packaging, which is&nbsp;leak-tight and impervious to battery fluid. The removed battery must also be protected from short circuits, be secured upright in its packaging, and be surrounded by compatible absorbent material that can sufficiently absorb its total liquid contents.</p>
<p>The packaging must be marked “BATTERY, WET, WITH WHEELCHAIR” or “BATTERY, WET, WITH MOBILITY AID”, and the “Corrosive” and “Package Orientation” labels must be attached.&nbsp;This completed package will be loaded in the cargo compartment. You will receive more information when you reach out to us to obtain the airline approval. </p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>



        </div>
</div>




                                
                                
                                
                                    

	
<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Personalandscientific">
    <h3>Personal and scientific</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Personal and scientific</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Chemical agent monitoring equipment</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>If you are a staff member of the Organization for the Prohibition of Chemical Weapons, on official travel, and you receive approval,&nbsp;you may carry chemical agent monitoring equipment. This includes a chemical agent monitor (CAM) and/or rapid alarm and identification device monitor (RAID-M), which does not have lithium batteries.</p>
<p>Please ensure that chemical agent monitoring equipment is securely packed. Instruments containing radioactive material must not exceed activity limits specified in Table 10.3.C of the IATA&nbsp;Dangerous Goods Regulations.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Using dry ice (Solid Carbon Dioxide) with perishable goods</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry a maximum of 2.5kg of dry ice with perishable goods that are not classified as dangerous goods, in packages that allow for the&nbsp;release of carbon dioxide gas, in your hand and checked baggage.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Packages containing dry ice, in checked baggage, must be marked with&nbsp;<span>the net weight of dry ice and be labelled “DRY ICE”.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Heat-producing items</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry heat-producing items such as underwater torches (diving lamps) and soldering irons.</p>
<p>If you carry battery-powered equipment capable of generating extreme heat, which would cause a fire if activated, such as underwater high-intensity lamps, the heat-producing component and the battery must be separated from each other.</p>
<p>This can be done through the removal of the heat-producing component, the battery or another component, such as the fuse. Any battery that has been removed must be protected against short circuits.&nbsp;The removed batteries must be taken in hand baggage.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a>&nbsp;for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Internal combustion or fuel cell engines</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>Engines and equipment containing internal combustion or fuel cell engines, are acceptable only when they are in compliance with below mentioned requirements.</p>
<p>The engine or the equipment must not contain any other dangerous goods and batteries. &nbsp;</p>
<p>The engine is powered by a fuel that does not meet the classification criteria of any class or division of the dangerous goods regulations ,or</p>
<p>The fuel tank of the vehicle, machine or other apparatus has never contained any fuel, or the fuel tank has been flushed and purged of vapours and adequate measures taken to nullify the hazard.</p>
<p>The passenger has to provide a written or electronic documentation stating that the flushing &amp; purging procedures have been followed.</p>
<p>The entire fuel system of the engine has no free liquid and all fuel lines are sealed or capped or securely connected to the machinery or the apparatus.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Matches and cigarette lighters</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>This item is only allowed when carried on the person</p>
<p>You may carry a box of matches or a small cigarette lighter that does not contain unabsorbed liquid fuel, other than liquefied gas, on your person for your individual use.&nbsp;Your cigarette lighter should require you to perform two independent actions to activate ignition. You also may not carry matches or cigarette lighters in your checked or hand baggage.&nbsp;</p>
<p>In addition, you may not carry lighter fuel and lighter refills on your person, in your checked baggage or in your hand baggage.&nbsp;Moreover, you may not carry “strike anywhere” matches, “blue flame” or “cigar” lighters.</p>
<p>Lighters powered by a lithium battery, such as “laser plasma lighters”, “tesla coil lighters”, “flux lighters”, “arc lighters” and “double arc lighters”, without a safety cap or other means of protection against unintentional activation are also prohibited.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Non-radioactive medicinal and toiletry items</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry non-radioactive medicinal and toiletry items, in your checked and hand baggage. These items include aerosols such as hairsprays, perfumes and colognes, and medicines containing alcohol.&nbsp;You may also carry non-flammable, non-toxic aerosols of Division 2.2, with no subsidiary hazard, for sporting or home use.</p>
<p>The total net quantity of non-radioactive medicinal and toiletry items, and non-flammable, non-toxic aerosols&nbsp;of Division 2.2, must not exceed 2kg or 2l. In addition, the net quantity of each item must not exceed 0.5kg or 0.5l.<br>
</p>
<p>Release valves on aerosols must be protected by a cap or other suitable means to prevent inadvertent release of the contents. Please note that additional restrictions may apply.</p>
<p>When carried in hand baggage, the quantities may be restricted further, due to other regulations, such as LAGs.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Permeation devices</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may carry permeation devices, for calibrating air quality monitoring equipment in your checked baggage. Please ensure that your devices comply with the requirement of IATA Dangerous Goods Regulations Special Provision A41.</p>
<p>Additional restrictions apply. <a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a> for more information.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Security-type equipment</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-blocked"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may not carry security-type equipment such as attaché cases, cash boxes, cash bags, etc, which incorporate dangerous goods such as pyrotechnic material and lithium batteries.</p>
<p>However, you may carry certain security-type equipment in your checked baggage, if the equipment complies with&nbsp;specific requirements.</p>
<p>Additional restrictions apply. <a href="https://www.qatarairways.com/en/help.html">Contact us</a> for more information.<br>

<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Powder">
    <h3>Powder</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Powder</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Powder-like substances</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-blocked"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may not carry powder-like substances in containers exceeding 350ml in your hand baggage, and any such substances will be subject to further screening. You may however, carry powder-like substance(s) in containers exceeding 350ml in your checked baggage.</p>
<p>The above restrictions do not apply to medically prescribed powder-like substances, baby formulas and human remains.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Duty-free purchases of powder-like substances must be placed in tightly sealed security tamper evident bags (STEB).</p>
<p>Restrictions on powder-like substances apply to passengers travelling to/from the below-mentioned countries:&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p><b>Australia</b></p>
<p>Passengers departing from an international airport in Australia. Customers travelling to Canberra via Sydney, when flying with Qatar Airways, will need to clear international transit security screening at Sydney.</p>
<p><b>New Zealand</b></p>
<p>Passengers departing from an international airport in New Zealand, including transfer passengers who pass through international screening points, in New Zealand.</p>
<p><b>Qatar</b></p>
<p>Passengers travelling on direct flights from Qatar to the United States of America.<br>
</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>



        </div>
</div>




                                
                                
                                
                                    

	
<div class="vt-rt-group" id="Securityrestricteditems">
    <h3>Security-restricted items</h3>
    <h3 class="mob_title"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span>Security-restricted items</h3>
        <div class="vt-rt-group-content">
        
        	




    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Blunt instruments</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-blocked"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may not carry blunt instruments that could cause serious injury when used to hit in the cabin of the aircraft, These items may be carried in your checked baggage. Examples of these instruments include:</p>
<p>- Baseball and softball bats</p>
<p>- Martial arts equipment</p>
<p>- Clubs and batons such as&nbsp;billy clubs, blackjacks and night sticks.</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Explosives and incendiary substances devices</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
            
       		 
            
        	
       			 <div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-exclamation"></span> Need approval</div>
       		 


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may not carry the following explosives and incendiary substances devices, including replicas, that could cause serious injury or threaten the safety of the aircraft, such as:</p>
<p>- Ammunition (may be carried in your checked baggage with permission).</p>
<p>- Blasting caps</p>
<p>- Detonators and fuses</p>
<p>- Mines, grenades and other explosive military stores</p>
<p>- Pyrotechnics, including fireworks</p>
<p>- Smoke-generating canisters or cartridges containing dynamite, gunpowder and plastic explosives</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Guns and firearms</h4>
    <div class="baggage-type">

        

		
			
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-checkmark1"></span> Checked baggage</div>
        	
            
       		 
            
        		<div class="bag-type"><span class="icon-blocked"></span> Hand baggage</div>
        	
        	


		



     </div>
     <div class="vt-subgroup-content">
         
         
        	<div class="vt-sg-desc"><p>You may not carry guns, firearms and other devices that discharge projectiles to cause serious injury, or items that could be mistaken for such devices, including toys, antiques and replicas in the cabin of the aircraft.&nbsp;The following items, however, can be placed in your checked baggage:</p>
<p>- Firearms of all types, including pistols, revolvers, rifles and shotguns (may be carried in your checked baggage with permission).</p>
<p>- Toy guns, replicas and imitations of firearms, which could be mistaken for real weapons</p>
<p>- Components of firearms excluding telescopic sights</p>
<p>- Compressed air and carbon dioxide guns, including pistols, pellet guns, rifles and ball-bearing guns</p>
<p>- Signal flare pistols and starter pistols</p>
<p>- Bows, cross bows and arrows</p>
<p>- Harpoon guns and spear guns</p>
<p>- Slingshots and catapults</p>
</div>
         
     </div>
     </div></div>


    
    
    <div class="verticaltabitem"><div class="vt-subgroup">
    <h4>Electro shock weapons and disabling devices</h4>

   <script>
       $(document).ready(function(){
      var $nodeName = "#table-module-OZZNO-table_copy_copy_copy .C6_1";
      var tableHeaders = [];

      $($nodeName).find('table').removeAttr("cellspacing cellpadding border width");
	  $($nodeName).find('table th').each(function(){
      	tableHeaders.push($(this).text());
      });

	  if ($(window).width() < 767) {
			$($nodeName).find('table tr').each(function(i){
				var $this = $(this);
				$(this).find('td').each(function(index){
					if($(this).attr('rowspan') != undefined){
						$($nodeName).find('table tr').eq(i+1).find('td').eq(index).before('<td>'+$(this).text()+'</td>');
					}
				});
			});
        	$($nodeName).find('th').parent().hide();
      }

	var $tableRows = $($nodeName).find('tr');
      $tableRows.each(function(){
          var t = 0;
          var $tableData = $(this).find('td');
          if($tableData != undefined && $tableData != '') {
      		$tableData.each(function(){
              if(tableHeaders[t] == '&nbsp;'){

              $(this).attr("data-th",'');
              }else {
                $(this).attr("data-th", tableHeaders[t]);
              }
			  if($(window).width() < 767){
					($(this).attr('data-th') != undefined && $(this).attr('data-th').length > 45) ? $(this).css('margin-bottom',($(this).attr('data-th').length/2)+20+'px') : $(this).css('margin-bottom','0');
				}

      		t++;
      
      });
          }

      });
      $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').css('text-align','');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('width');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('valign');
});
   </script>
