<script type="text/javascript">
	
	 var directionVal;
	 var textpositionDesktop = "left";
	 var textpositionMobile = "left";
	 var textposition = textpositionDesktop;
	 var C1HeroImageTeadDropNode = "heroimage_teardrop_s";
	 var parentElement = '.heroimage-teardrop-desktop';
	 if(($(window).width() <= 750) && $('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').length){
		parentElement = '.heroimage-teardrop-mobile';
		textposition = textpositionMobile;
	 }
	 if(C1HeroImageTeadDropNode==""){
	 	 C1HeroImageTeadDropNode = "imagery1";
	 }
	 var $C1TearDropHeaderImage = $(parentElement+' .'+C1HeroImageTeadDropNode);
	 var $C1TearDropMobileImageURL = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('mobile-image');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImageURL = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('desktop-image');
	 var $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-mobile-fadeColor');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-desktop-fadeColor');
	 var $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg =  $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('bg');
	 var $mobileImagedataBg = $C1TearDropHeaderImage.data('mobile-bg');
	 var $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop  = true;
	 var $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = true;
	 var directionType = $('#fadeValue').val();
	if(directionType == "qr.arabic"){
         if(textposition == "left" || textposition == "center") {
   		 	directionVal =  "to left";
         }
         else {
			directionVal =  "to right";
         }
     } 
     else {

         if(textposition == "left" || textposition == "center") {
   		 	directionVal =  "to right";
         }
         else {
			directionVal =  "to left";
         }
     }

    $(document).ready(function() {

    imageLoad();

    });

	$(window).on('load',function(){
    imageLoad();

    });


function imageLoad() {


        if($C1TearDropMobileImageURL =='url();'){

        $C1TearDropMobileImageURL=$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL;
        $mobileImagedataBg = $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg;
        $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor =$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor;

   		}

		if($(window).width() <= 750){
			if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile)
			{
				if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
		   		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
		   		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
		  		}else{
		  	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
		 	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL);
                    $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		  		}

				$C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = false;
			}else
			{
				if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
               		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
		  		}else{
		  	 		$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'");');
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
		  		}


           	}

        }else {
         	if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop)
			{
				if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL+'background-size: cover');
				}else{
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropDesktopImageURL);
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
				}

				$C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop= false;
			}else
           	{
				if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');
				}else{
					$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:url("'+$C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg+'");');
                     $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
				}


			 }

        }
        $(window).on('resize', function(){
			if($(this).width() <= 750){

				if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile)
				{
					if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%),'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL+'background-size: cover');
					}else{
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $mobileImagedataBg);
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:'+$C1TearDropMobileImageURL);
                        $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
					}

					$C1TearDropFirstTimeMobile = false;
				}else
				{
					if($C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('style', 'background-image:linear-gradient('+directionVal+','+$C1TearDropMobileImageFadeColor+' ,transparent 100%), url("'+$mobileImagedataBg+'"); background-size: cover ');

                        $("div.promotional-text-base").addClass("drop-shaddow");
					}


				}
			}else {

				if( $C1TearDropFirstTimeDesktop)
				{
					if($C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != undefined && $C1TearDropDesktopImageFadeColor != ""){
						$C1TearDropHeaderImage.attr('data-bg', $C1TearDropDesktopImagedataBg);

	if($(window).width() <= 750){
		if($('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').length){
			$('.heroimage-teardrop-mobile').removeAttr('hidden');

});

    <div class="row">

It is also used to specify the conditions under which re-routings may take place or tickets may be re-issued or refunded.</p>

<div class="table section">



   
   
   
      <div class="tableComp tableContainer" id="table-module-IG6E8-table_copy">
         
   <div class="C6_1 row" id="table">
      <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12">
         
         <table>
<tbody><tr><td><p>Before Departure</p>
</td>
<td><p>The definition refers to the first flight of the pricing unit or before utilization of the first coupon of the ticket.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>After Departure</p>
</td>
<td><p>The definition refers to the subsequent flights of the Pricing unit or after utilization of the first coupon of the ticket.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Voluntary Change</p>
</td>
<td><p>If any change made to the originating flight/routing/date by the passenger</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Involuntary Change</p>
</td>
<td><p>Involuntary rerouting situation occurs when a passenger is forced to change carrier, and/or routing and/or class and/or type of fare that on which the passenger was due to fly due to a change by one or more airlines in the itinerary.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Refund/Cancellation Charges</p>
</td>
<td><p>The repayment to the purchaser of all or a portion of a fare rate or charge for unused carriage or service.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Revalidation</p>
</td>
<td><p>Acceptance of an electronic ticket by the intended validating carrier of the ticket constitutes validation. There can be no change to origin, destination, stopover/ connecting points or fare (RBD) (not permitted for agencies)</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Re-Issue</p>
</td>
<td><p>Alteration to a ticket that cannot be done through revalidation and requires the issuance of a new ticket. Issuance of a new ticket against a previously issued ticket, in accordance with the provisions of voluntary rerouting for partially used pricing units.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Rerouting</p>
</td>
<td><p>Change of routing and/or other changes which require ticket reissuance. Except as otherwise specifically defined in a rule, it is recommended that with respect to a passenger, rerouting means a change of route, fare, carrier, type of aircraft, class of service, flight or validity from that originally provided in the appropriate transportation document.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Ticket Validity</p>
</td>
<td><p>Contract between an airline and a customer which is valid for a maximum period of 12 months from the date of issue for the specified journey. The outbound flight must be taken within 12 months from the date of issue .The inbound flight(s) may be no longer than the actual fare validity permits however the ticket validity is independent of the fare validity.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Fare Validity</p>
</td>
<td><p>Fare validity is defined as the maximum period within which travel can be performed for a given fare. For each fare, validity is driven by the maximum stay rule of the fare rule/condition. Any fare governed by a maximum stay rule may however be upgraded to a higher fare level with longer maximum stay (never to exceed the 12 months of ticket validity) with payment of applicable fare difference and change fee. In case of combination the most restrictive fare rules will be used, i.e. (6M+3M) 3 months will be used.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>No-Show Charge</p>
</td>
<td><p>The charge made by reason of the failure of a passenger to use reserved accommodation, either through failure to arrive at the airport at the time fixed by the carrier, or through arriving improperly documented or otherwise not ready to travel on flight.&nbsp;</p>
<p>No show can be considered due to the following reasons:</p>
<ul>
<li>A passenger who fails to use reserved accommodation for reason other than misconnection&nbsp;</li>
<li>A passenger is denied check in due to not having passport, Valid visa etc. in correct order to be transported.</li>
<li>A passenger fails to show to the flight before the gate is closed unless delay is due to connecting flight being delayed where in the entire itinerary is present on one or conjunctive QR document(s).</li>
<li>A passenger fails to change/cancel his/her reservation 3 hours prior to departure</li>
<li>Any re-booking made within 3 hours prior to departure or after departure of flight as shown in the e-ticket will be considered as a No-show.&nbsp;</li>
<li>For a scenario where in the original reservation is cancelled prior to No-show condition, but the new reservation are made after departure of the flight (as mentioned in e-ticket coupon) QR Reservation and Ticketing Staff may perform a manual transaction (without ATC entries) to avoid the collection of No-show fee.</li>
</ul>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Partially Utilized Ticket</p>
</td>
<td><p>When a minimum of one flight coupon of an e-ticket is used (flown) is considered as partially utilized ticket.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Fully Unutilized Ticket</p>
</td>
<td><p>When all the flight coupons of an e-ticket are open for use is considered as fully unutilized ticket.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Residual Value</p>
</td>
<td><p>When a reissue/exchange or rerouting of an e-ticket results in a lower fare/tax(es) the balance amount due to the passenger between the originally paid fare/tax(es) and the new fare/tax(es) is termed as Residual Value.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Fare Component / Fare Break Point</p>
</td>
<td><p>A portion of an itinerary between two consecutive fare construction points. If the journey has only one fare component, the points of origin and destination are the only fare construction points.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Pricing Unit</p>
</td>
<td><p>A journey or a part of a journey which is priced as a separate entity, i.e. is capable of being ticketed separately.</p>
</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr><tr><td><p>Side Trip Combination</p>
</td>
<td><p>Combination of a pricing unit at an en-route point of a fare component.</p>

</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
</tr></tbody></table>

      </div>
   </div>

   <script>
       $(document).ready(function(){
      var $nodeName = "#table-module-IG6E8-table_copy .C6_1";
      var tableHeaders = [];

      $($nodeName).find('table').removeAttr("cellspacing cellpadding border width");
	  $($nodeName).find('table th').each(function(){
      	tableHeaders.push($(this).text());
      });

	  if ($(window).width() < 767) {
			$($nodeName).find('table tr').each(function(i){
				var $this = $(this);
				$(this).find('td').each(function(index){
					if($(this).attr('rowspan') != undefined){
						$($nodeName).find('table tr').eq(i+1).find('td').eq(index).before('<td>'+$(this).text()+'</td>');
					}
				});
			});
        	$($nodeName).find('th').parent().hide();
      }

	var $tableRows = $($nodeName).find('tr');
      $tableRows.each(function(){
          var t = 0;
          var $tableData = $(this).find('td');
          if($tableData != undefined && $tableData != '') {
      		$tableData.each(function(){
              if(tableHeaders[t] == '&nbsp;'){

              $(this).attr("data-th",'');
              }else {
                $(this).attr("data-th", tableHeaders[t]);
              }
			  if($(window).width() < 767){
					($(this).attr('data-th') != undefined && $(this).attr('data-th').length > 45) ? $(this).css('margin-bottom',($(this).attr('data-th').length/2)+20+'px') : $(this).css('margin-bottom','0');
				}

      		t++;
      
      });
          }

      });
      $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').css('text-align','');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('width');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('valign');
});
   </script>

                              <li id="poi-tab-YICT6" class="fade in all">                              	
                                 <div class="slide-content-container tab-item-2">
								 
					<!-- For Mobile view accordion tabs-->
	        <div class="container">
              <div class="row d-flex d-md-none header_content">
                <div class="col">
                    <div class="convert_mobile_btn">

          <div class="card_detail_content">
                                       <div class="logotext-partner section">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>Adding and Changing Segments to an Existing Reservation</b></p>
<p>There can be numerous reasons why a passenger requests to make changes in his/her itinerary. All changes to reservations should be handled as if these were original requests for reservations. Amending reservation office carrying out amendments must verify if passenger holds any other reservations as well and if so, determine if they are still needed.</p>
<p>In order to give QR opportunity to resell all unwanted seats, minimize no-shows and maximize revenue, all such unwanted space (O&amp;D) must be cancelled immediately.</p>
<p>As QR is in O&amp;D environment, all amendments leading to new O&amp;D must be followed. This include but is not limited to cancellation of old O&amp;D and followed by:</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Rebooking or rerouting of entire O&amp;D</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Rebooking or rerouting of particular flight from O&amp;D</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Cancelling</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Upgrading of entire O&amp;D to higher cabin (revenue and redemption upgrade)</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Upgrading of particular flight from O&amp;D to higher cabin (revenue and redemption upgrade)</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Booking additional sectors to O&amp;D resulting in new O&amp;D</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Amendments leading to stopovers</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Amendments leading to side-trips and being ticketed separately</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Combinations of above scenarios</li>
</ul>
<p>Booking additional sectors or side trips which finally do not affect existing O&amp;D, do not require cancellation of old O&amp;D. Any new side-trip being ticketed separately and irrespective of any or nil effect on existing O&amp;Ds, should be booked and ticketed in separate PNR with cross-reference remark containing reference RLOC.</p>
<p>Qatar Airways Reservation &amp; Inventory system is able to offer, when available, immediate confirmation of flights and booking classes required. This confirmation would be based on availability calculated on Origin &amp; Destination (O&amp;D) logic.</p>
<p><br>
However, availability of booking class for particular O&amp;D connection is also based on Point of Commencement (POC) decision or Origin &amp; Destination is considered as continuous journey from point of Origin to point of Destination. Simply, where the passenger begins and ends his or her journey. O&amp;D can be distinguished into three specific scenarios:</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><b>Local O&amp;D</b>&nbsp;which involves a single nonstop leg (DOH QR DEL).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><b>Online O&amp;D</b>&nbsp;as a portion of the journey that traverses QR network (IAD QR X/DOH QR BKK). Includes certain code-share itineraries, where QR flight is operated by code-share partner airline.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><b>Trip O&amp;D</b>&nbsp;is regardless of airlines involved and includes interline segments (ATL DL X/MAD QR X/DOH QR DXB)</li>
</ul>
<p>When QR segments are sold together in this way or on point-to-point basis (if seats are available on O&amp;D level), they are known as married segments. If segments are married together in PNR, it may not be possible to cancel, price or ticket a segment individually and will be treated as one unit by the GDS/CRS.</p>
<p><br>
Marriage Segment Control prevents using flight connections to sell local flights that would not be available if requested outside that connection. QR Revenue Management System (RMS) is capable to identify bypass practices and rejects any cancel request in case the remaining proportion of the O&amp;D is not available. Similarly, any bypass of point-to-point sell is detectable by RMS and rejects any onward/inward sell request in case of unavailability of seats on O&amp;D level.</p>

                    
                    
                </div>
            </div>

		



    </div>

    </div>

										<div class="accordion-module-item">
											<button type="button" class="accordion-module-opener">
                                                
                                                ATC Penalties Policy FAQs
											<span class="accessibility-state" data-accessibility-state="" data-accessibility-active="Opened" data-accessibility-inactive="Closed">Closed</span></button>
												<div class="accordion-module-content-holder collapse" aria-expanded="false" style="height: 0px;">
													<div class="accordion-module-content clearfix" tabindex="">
														




    
    
    <div class="logotext-partner">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>What is ATC ?</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
</ul>
<p>ATC stands for Amadeus Ticket Changer. ATC allows you to automatically recalculate and prepare documents for the issuance of voluntary reissue/exchange, and to process refunds of electronic&nbsp; tickets based on the IATA industry standard.</p>
<p><b>What can ATC handle?</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>All E-tickets</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Multi-carrier, partner Interline tickets</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Issued by any Point of Sales</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Unused or partially used tickets</li>
</ul>
<p><b>What fare types</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Public fares</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Most Private fares</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Amadeus Nego fares</li>
</ul>
<p><b>The types of changes</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Itinerary</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Date, Flight and Booking Class changes</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Including multi passengers PNRs</li>
</ul>
<p><b>The rules for ATC re-issuance</b></p>
<p>All tickets are eligible for an unlimited number of reissue/exchange at any time, except when a ticket has already been reissued after departure in another Global Distribution System (GDS).</p>
<p>Once you have made the necessary modifications to the passenger itinerary and entered the pricing entries, the system will process the best pricing solution, according to the reissue/exchange conditions for a reissue/exchange.</p>
<p>A reissue/exchange generates a new ticket including penalties, i.e.; Change of reservation fee and/or No-show fee (if any). The penalties are collected under tax code ‘XP’. It creates a residual value EMD TSM-P if there is any amount due to the passenger.</p>
<p>The Office profile must be updated to use ATC.</p>
<p>The ticket number of the document to be reissued or exchanged must be present in the PNR (FH/FA element). If not present, it must be entered manually in the PNR or in the ATC pricing entry.</p>
<p>The e-ticket record of the original document must be accessible for Amadeus to retrieve the data that is required by ATC to perform the Voluntary reissue/exchange. If Amadeus is not allowed to retrieve the e-ticket record, the following error message is displayed by the system:</p>
<p><b>Can ATC be used on Voluntary changes?</b></p>
<p>Yes, ATC can be used on voluntary changes for all QR market fares filed in the GDS.</p>
<p><b>Can ATC be used on involuntary changes?</b></p>
<p>ATC only facilitates in copying the Fare details related to involuntary transaction, However , subsequent re-issuance needs to be handled manually and has to be validated by the ticketing agents , for involuntary changes the general rules for re-issuance and revalidation are as mentioned below.</p>
<p>Routing has changed - reissue/exchange</p>
<p>Flight number has changed -&nbsp;reissue/exchange</p>
<p>RBD has changed -&nbsp;reissue/exchange</p>
<p>Date of travel has changed -&nbsp; reissue/exchange.</p>
<p><b>Can ATC be used on un-published fares (paper fares)?</b></p>
<p>No, all transaction on un-published fares are to be handled manually, adhering to the penalties policy implemented in the network effective 15th June, 2013.</p>
<p><b>Does the penalties policy apply to both voluntary and in-voluntary changes?</b></p>
<p>No, the penalties policy implemented effective 15th of June 2013 applies to only voluntary changes,</p>
<p><b>Is revalidation allowed on changes?</b></p>
<p>revalidations not permitted, e<span style="background-color: transparent;">ven tickets eligible for free-of-charge (FOC) changes need to be reissued/exchanged by the respective travel agencies.</span></p>
<p><b>Effective when can ATC be used in respective POSs?</b></p>
<p>ATC should only be used by POSs on tickets issued on or after the date of implementation in their POSs, (journeys originating in your POS). Implementation dates for ATC by region are as follows.</p>
<p>Qatar. 27th May 2013</p>
<p>GCCLI: 15th June 2013</p>
<p>ISC &amp; EASWP: 15th June 2013.</p>
<p>NSW Europe &amp; Eastern Europe: 5th August 2013</p>
<p>Africa: 15th August 2013</p>
<p>Americas 31st of August 2013.</p>
<p><b>Effective when can ATC be used for journeys origination outside concerned POS?</b></p>
<p>Effective when ATC is implemented throughout the QR network.</p>
<p><b>Can Travel Agents use ATC?</b></p>
<p>Effective 27th January 2015, Amadeus ticket changes functionality is available to travel agents using Amadeus GDS for any Qatar Airways e-tickets.</p>
<p><b>What is not covered/out of scope of ATC and the penalties document implemented?</b></p>
<p>All involuntary changes.</p>
<p>Fares not files in GDSs.</p>
<p>IATA fares and OAL fare not filed by QR.</p>
<p>Tickets that have been revalidated for FCR, FFP, staffs travel tickets.</p>
<p><b>Can ATC be used when ticketing service fee applies?</b></p>
<p>ATC can be used for re-issuance transaction, however ticketing service fee needs to be added manually under tax code XP.</p>


                    
                    
                </div>
            </div>

		



    </div>

                              <li id="poi-tab-S05P2" class="fade in all">                              	
                                 <div class="slide-content-container tab-item-3">
								 
					<!-- For Mobile view accordion tabs-->
	        <div class="container">
              <div class="row d-flex d-md-none header_content">
                <div class="col">
                    <div class="convert_mobile_btn">
                        <div class="d-flex d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                    
                              
                        </div>
                        <span class="icon-ic_nav_chevron-down d-inline-block"></span>
                    </div>

			<!-- For Mobile view accordion tabs close -->
          <div class="card_detail_content">
                                       <div class="logotext-partner section">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>Applicability - Changes (Re-issuance/exchange)</b></p>
<p><b>Before Departure:</b></p>
<p>Change penalty before departure will be charged or No-show charges (if any) and the ticket needs to be re-issued/exchnaged with applicable fare difference (if any).</p>
<p>When voluntary change occurs irrespective of the outbound or inbound flight of the journey the fare will be recalculated applying new fares/rules (adhering to the new AP condition) in effect on the date of the re-issue/exchange</p>
<p><b>After Departure:</b></p>
<p>Change Penalty after departure will be charged or No-show charges (if any) and the ticket needs to be Re-issued/exchnaged.</p>
<p>New fare will be recalculated using fares in effect on the date when the original ticket was issued. Highest penalty charges among of the changed fare components will be applied.</p>
<p><b>Genral Conditions:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>a) Changes are applicable only if the fare rule allows change of reservation.<br>
</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>b) Change fee applies per transaction.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>c) Change / No-show fee must be coded as XP in the tax field</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>d) In case of No-show only one fee to be charged. Either no-show or change fee whichever is higher.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>e) For No-show scenarios please refer to No-show definition</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>f) Revalidation is not permitted on QR Market fares (published, private and paper fares). For any change scenario ticket reissuance is mandatory irrespective of any ADC or NO ADC.</li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Exception </b>– For group PNR’s tickets issued by travel agencies with passive segment using GDS other than Amadeus; revalidation is permitted to associate a ticket number to group PNR. Any ADC collection, ticket has to be reissued adhering to the group policy</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>g) <b>Rerouting:</b> When there is a change in Fare Break Point where the new route results in a lower fare. The residual amount can be refunded to the passenger through the original form of payment or EMD as transportation credit voucher.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>h) <b>Re-pricing rule:</b> New ticket has to be equal or higher than previous ticket fare value, when change in seasonality / weekday / weekend fares results in a lower fare, the residual value should remain as nonrefundable:</li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left: 80.0px;">i) Penalties (Change / No-show / re-issuance charges) will be applied as per the highest of all changed fare component(s).</p>
<p style="margin-left: 80.0px;">ii) Penalty Charge applies for Adult, Child and infant occupying a seat. Charge (including No-Show charge) will not apply for infant not occupying a seat.</p>
<p style="margin-left: 80.0px;"><span style="background-color: transparent;">This implies that child and infant occupying a seat will pay the same change / cancelation penalties as adult passenger.&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="margin-left: 80.0px;">iii) If a passenger is denied check in due to not having, passport, and/or valid Visa in correct order to be transported - Applicable Change penalties and No-show charges have to be collected.</p>
<p style="margin-left: 80.0px;">iv) For Non-refundable fares if the passenger is a No-show and the fare rule allows changes with No-show penalties, then re-issuance to new travel date is permitted (within ticket validity) after collecting the applicable penalties however refund of any residual value on such tickets will not be permitted.</p>
<p><b style="background-color: transparent;">Change Fee - Collection Scenarios</b><br>
</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><b>a) Date Change is done for Outbound only.</b></li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Example: If O/B change fee is USD 100 and I/B is USD 125, highest fee of changed fare component(s) (USD 100) will apply for the transaction.</li>
</ul>

<p><b>b) Date change is done for Inbound only.</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Example: If O/B change fee is USD 100 and I/B is USD 125, highest fee of the changed fare component(s) (USD 125) will apply for the transaction.</li>
</ul>

<p><b>c) Date change is done for both direction in one transaction.<br>
</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Example: If O/B change fee is USD 100 and I/B is USD 125, highest fee of the changed fare component(s) (USD 125) will apply for the transaction.</li>
</ul>

<p><b>d) If Change of Reservation is Not Permitted in a pricing unit:<br>
</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>In a combination of fares scenario, if one of the changed fare components does not allow Change of reservation: No change of reservation allowed for that fare component only.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Example: For scenario of&nbsp;O/B before departure of flight, O/B fare component rule do not permit Changes and I/B fare rule allows changes, possible change is only for I/B fare component.</li>
</ul>

<p><b>Voluntary Upgrades / Downgrades / Upsell / Downsell Scenarios:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>A change of reservation may result in voluntary upgrades / downgrades (between cabins) and inventory upsell / downsell (within same cabin). “Difference in fare calculation” for such scenarios will be from Origin to Destination (OnD) as per the applied Fare Break Point on the ticket. Segment based upgrade / downgrade / upsell / downsell within a fare component of a journey is not permitted (e.g. OnD LONBKK journey, upgrade required on LONDOH only).</li>
</ul>
<p><b>a) Voluntary Upgrades:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Upgrade between Cabins: (Y to J/F, J to F) at any time within the ticket validity fares can be upgraded to any fare in the higher cabin on OnD basis.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>reissue/exchange and change fee will not be applicable however additional tax(es) (if any) have to be collected.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If the voluntary cabin upgrade happens within 3 hours prior to departure of flight no-show penalty will not be charged. No-show charge applies if the change is made after departure of flight as shown on the e-ticket coupon.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If the reissued/exchanged ticket is subsequently changed the conditions of the reissued/exchanged fare will be applicable.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>b) Inventory Upsell within same Cabin:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Any time within the ticket validity the fare can be reissued/exchanged to any higher fare in the same cabin, and then the fare will be recalculated from the point of origin provided the conditions of the higher fare have been met and applicable difference in fare is collected.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>reissue/exchange/change fee will be applicable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>No-show penalty applies for 3 hours prior to departure of flight.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If the reissued/exchanged ticket is subsequently changed the conditions of the reissued/exchanged fare will be applicable.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>c) Voluntary Downgrades between Cabins (J/F to Y, F to J):&nbsp;</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Downgrades between (J/F to Y, F to J) at any time within the Ticket validity Fares can be downgraded to any fare in lower cabin and then the fare will be recalculated from point of origin provided conditions of the lower cabin fare have been met.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Re-issue and change fee will be applicable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If the voluntary cabin downgrade is happening within 3 hours prior to departure of flight No-show penalty will be charged.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If the Re-issued ticket is subsequently changed the conditions of the re-issued fare will be applicable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Any residual value as result of cabin downgrade will remain as non-refundable.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>d) Inventory Downsell:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Within same cabin is not permitted in all scenarios including change in fare break point.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Combination of Fares:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Highest penalty of all fare components within the changed pricing units of the ticketed journey applies. After identifying pricing units on the ticketed journey that contains “changed fare components”, the highest charge amount of all changed fare components within those pricing units will be applicable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Itinerary with multiple pricing units (end-on-end combinations/side trips):&nbsp;“Change of reservation not permitted” condition applies specifically to the pricing units having fare components with changes not permitted.&nbsp; Respective penalties for other pricing units apply.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>System Date Range Limitation:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Reservation can be made for a maximum of 360 days from the date of issue. For such journeys if the inbound date of travel is beyond 360 days (out of system date range).</li>
</ul>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><u><i>*Note: other GDS systems may have different system range limitations:</i></u></div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Amadeus </b>- 361 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Sabre </b>- 362 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Abacus</b>-362 days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Travelport </b>-&nbsp;362 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Worlspan&nbsp;</b>- 362 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Galileo&nbsp;</b>- 362 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Infini </b>- 362 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Sirena&nbsp; </b>- 330 Days</div>
<div style="margin-left: 40.0px;"><b>Travelsky</b> - 361&nbsp; days</div>
</div>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>First change of reservation will be permitted free of charge for the inbound fare component irrespective of the change of reservation condition in the fare rule.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Endorsement box should mention “1FOC for travel date out of system date range”.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Once the travel date is within the system date range ticket has to be re-issued availing 1 FOC. The change must always be to a date later than the original booking and more than 360 days (Amadeus) from the issuance of the ticket. Otherwise FOC change does not apply and ADM will be raised for incorrect application. This exception will not be applicable if fare rule allows any free change of reservation.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>This process has to be handled manually as this is out of ATC scope.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Segments with date of travel out of system range:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>One rebooking penalty waiver is permitted for rebooking in the same RBD, provided Fare Basis rules are adhered. Any rebooking on date specified in Endorsements/Restrictions field which results to higher fare, taxes, fees, sur-/charges subject to that additional collection (e.g. due to RBD change, change from week to weekend fare, travel restrictions, blackouts, seasonality. Min/max stay, etc…) and Fare Basis rules to be adhered. Service Fee, sometimes called as Ticketing Fee or OB Fee can be waived.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>In case that original RBD is not available, you may rebook based on the standard voluntary principle and collect difference of fare, taxes, fees, sur-/charges as applicable for the actual date of travel specified in Endorsements/Restrictions field (DDMMMYYYY). Rebooking penalty can be waived once and fare basis rules shall be adhered. Service Fee, sometimes called as Ticketing Fee or OB Fee can be waived.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>In case of any date change, rebooking penalty and Service Fee, sometimes called as Ticketing Fee or OB Fee are not waived.&nbsp;</li>
</ul>


                    
                    
                </div>
            </div>

		



    </div>

          <div class="card_detail_content">
                                       <div class="logotext-partner section">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>Refund Description :</b></p>
<p>Refund is the repayment to the purchaser of all or a portion of a fare, rate or charge for unused carriage or service.</p>
<p>If a ticket is non-refundable, no part of the fare and surcharges (YQ/YR) will be refunded. However for markets where YQ &amp; YR has to be refunded as per local government's regulatory requirement, supporting documents have to be submitted for&nbsp;approval and fare conditions should reflect this.</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If a ticket is issued with non-refundable fare(s); unutilized coupon's flown based tax(es) are refundable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If non-refundable fare is re-issued to a refundable fare, YQ / YR and the base fare of the original non-refundable ticket remains as non-refundable</li>
</ul>
<p><b>However there are instances wherein ticket refund requests for restricted documents may entertained due to unavoidable circumstances as below and at the discretion of QR commercial management:</b></p>
<p><b style="background-color: transparent;">1</b><span style="background-color: transparent;">. Passengers holding confirmed QR tickets may not be able to travel on flights due to following reasons:</span><br>
</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>QR flight is delayed and passenger arranges an alternative flight on his/her own and not the option provided by QRFailure to operate a flight reasonably accordingly to schedule and aircraft changes</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Passenger or a Near Relative (please refer QR conditions of carriage for applicability) suffers from a terminal illness prior to flight departure, a valid medical certificate to be submitted.&nbsp;</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Failure to operate a flight due to extraordinary events or circumstances classified under Force Majeure or Act of God. These conditions include but are not limited to flooding, extreme weather conditions, earthquake, tsunami, hurricane, volcanic eruption, war, political unrest, strike, riot etc. A QR Commercial Policy will be issued to cover extraordinary event/circumstance and serve as basis to authorize refunds.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Some customers may not get visa to enter Doha. Qatar immigration authorities can deny visa to Qatar Airways customers.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>2</b>. Ticket refund may also be necessitated due to system/printing related errors.</p>
<p><b>3</b>. Passengers declared as "blacklisted" are not allowed to travel on QR flights. Ticket is suspended in such cases, ticket and other costs are refunded to these passengers.</p>
<p>In situations where&nbsp;your passenger misses a flight as a result of QR’s fault, the no-show charges will not be applied upon verification of such situations.</p>

<p>Refund validity of ticket is 12 months from date of issue for fully unused ticket; and 12 months from the first uplift date for a partially used ticket.</p>
<p><b>Note:</b></p>
<p>Refund of tickets beyond 12 months is only allowed in the following situations:</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>1) Local law / regulatory requirements: When local regulatory requirements take precedence over Qatar Airways Ticket Refund Policy, local station finance is authorized to process the refund on such scenarios without any subsequent approval.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>2) Refund in case of death: Legal heirs of the deceased will be refunded after valid documentation (Death certificate or copy etc.) is verified.</li>
</ul>
<p>Please coordinate refund requests to your local Qatar Airways office.</p>

<p><b>Refunds in another Country</b></p>
<p>With the implementation of electronic tickets (E-tickets) and other instruments such as Electronic Miscellaneous Documents (EMDs), the existing electronic environment now offers much more flexibility towards processing of refunds in countries other than point of sale (POS).</p>
<p>Some countries have regulations in place that prohibit sales made in those countries to be refunded in other countries. Where such regulations exist, Qatar Airways will continue to ensure compliance.</p>
<p>Restrictions to refund outside the country of sale are implemented in the following countries namely:</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Algeria</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>India</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Greece</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>France/Benelux</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Brazil</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Morocco</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Nigeria</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Tunis</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Iran</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Malawi</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Eritrea</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Sudan</li>
</ul>

<div class="logotext-partner section">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>Applicability - Cancellation / Refund</b></p>
<p><b>Before Departure</b></p>
<p>For fully unutilized ticket the amount paid will be fully refunded including tax(es) after deducting the cancellation charges (if any) as per fare rules provided the fare is refundable.</p>
<p><b>After Departure</b></p>
<p>For fares which permits refund after departure.</p>
<p>For partially utilized ticket the refund will be the amount equal to the difference between the fare paid and the OW applicable fare for travel between the points for which the ticket has been used less any cancellation fees. If one way fare is not available or published on the inventory mentioned on the ticket then deduct next available OW in higher RBD for which the journey has been performed.</p>
<p><b>Filing Process:</b></p>
<p>For calculating the refund automatically under ATC transaction, ATPCO CAT–33 is coded with a booking class mapping to pick the next available OW in the absence of a published OW on the same RBD. Whenever there is a change to the existing OW structure, (example publishing new OW’s in lower RBD’s, or withdrawing OW’s from existing structure) Station Pricing has to notify the Fare distribution team to ensure the CAT-33 coding is done correctly and the same has to be validated at the time of publishing fares.<br>
</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>i) If applicable OW fare plus cancellation fees exceed the actual collected base fare for the journey, the base fare paid remains non-refundable. All unutilized coupons flown based tax (es) excluding YQ/YR will be refundable for such scenarios.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>ii) Tickets which are used beyond point of Turnaround – No Refund permitted.<br>
</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>iii) Tickets which are used out of sequence – No Refund permitted.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>iv) Unutilized or partially flown tickets with non refundable taxes should remain as non refundable.</li>
</ul>
<p><i>*Note: If the cancellation penalty is higher than the ticketed fare then cancellation penalty will deduct from YQ/YR manually”</i></p>
<p><b style="background-color: transparent;">Cancellation / Refund Scenarios - General Conditions</b><br>
</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If a fare is non-refundable then no part of the Fare + YQ/YR will be refundable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Charge applies for Adult, Child and infant occupying a seat.&nbsp; Charge (including No-Show charge) will not apply for infant not occupying a seat. This implies that child and infant occupying a seat will pay the same change / cancellation penalties as adult passenger.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Change / No-show Fee collected under XP in the tax field will remain as non-refundable.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>In case of no-show only one fee to be charged. Either no-show or cancellation fee whichever is higher</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>For no-show scenarios please refer to no-show definition.<br>
</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Where a ticket is issued with a combination of at least two fare basis, (e.g. Promotional fares combined with a Flexi fares) the most restrictive rules will apply.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If a passenger was denied check-in for not having valid travel documents (Passport, Visa, etc.) – all applicable cancellation and no-show fees should be collected.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Refund will be refused if the application is made after expiry of the ticket validity.&nbsp;</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If a ticket has been reissued/exchanged multiple times and finally submitted for cancellation, the highest cancellation fee / non-refundable amount among all the reissued/exchanged fares will apply.</li>
</ul>
<p><b>Cancellation Scenario on Combination of Multiple Fare Basis:</b></p>
<p><b>Totally unutilized tickets - Passenger is No-Show on O/B:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">

</ul>

<p><b>Non-Refundable Fares Scenarios:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">

<div class="logotext-partner section">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>Offloading After Cancellation:</b></p>
<p>Whenever segments are to be cancelled, rebooked or refunded 48 hours to 3 hours prior to departure, Travel Agent should check if e-ticket coupon :</p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Airport Control&nbsp; "A" - Control of the coupon has been sent from QR Reservation System Either to departure Control System or to Other Airline&nbsp; (operating carrier of code-share flight&nbsp; or interlinecarrier).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Checked in "C" - PAssenger is checked in and entitled to board the aircraft.</li>
</ul>

<p>Some GDSs may show A status or ARPT, in such case it is recommended to verify with the nearest QR Office or Customer Contact Center on whether the coupon has been checked-in.</p>
<p>In case coupon has been checked-in, passenger will have to be offloaded prior rebooking, reissue/exchange or refund. Simple segment cancellation will not offload passenger from check-in system and will treat passenger as no-show. In such case Travel Agent may be at risk of receiving ADM due to no-show.</p>

<p><b>How to offload passenger?</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If passenger did online check-in, then offload will have to be done via qatarairways.com.&nbsp;</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>If passenger did airport check-in, then offload will have to be done by airport team.</li>
</ul>

<p><b>Important note&nbsp;</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Offload can be done latest by 3 hours prior to departure, in order to rebook, reissue/exchange or refund e-ticket.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>E-ticket will lose its validity and will be suspended should offloading occur in less than 3 hours prior to departure. In such case, e-ticket can`t be rebooked, reissued/exchanged or refunded and a new e-ticket will have to be purchased.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>In case of refund, Travel Agent has to ensure that all coupons being refunded have been changed to R (RFND) status.</li>
</ul>

                    
                    
                </div>
            </div>

		



    </div>

    </div>

	var ulTag = $(".whitefontP").find("ul").addClass('bulleted-list');

          <div class="card_detail_content">
                                       <div class="logotext-partner section">





 

    <div class="whitefont" id="logotext-partner" style="background-color:inherit !important;margin-bottom: 30px;margin-top: 30px;">
       	
    <div class="row">
		 
         
            <div class="col-xs-12 qtr-txt-maroon">
			   
                
			    
                
				
                <div class="whitefontP">
                    <p><b>Reasons Causing No Show :</b></p>

<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Passengers, booking offices and travel agents failing to cancel unwanted reservations.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Missed connections due to flight delays</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Customers holding invalid personal and/or travel documents</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Communication mishandling</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Passengers holding reservations for more than one reservationfor the same services requirement "multiple or duplicate" bookings.</li>
</ul>

<p><b>Consequences to an itinerary in case of no show :</b></p>

<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>In case a customer is a no-show on a flight then all down-line segments of that itinerary are cancelled, <i>*certain regulatory exceptions apply.&nbsp;&nbsp;</i></li>
</ul>

<p><b>No show applies for the following scenarios:</b></p>
<ul class="bulleted-list">
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>A passenger who fails to use reserved accommodation for reason other than misconnection.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>A passenger is denied check in due to not having passport, valid visa etc. in order to be transported.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>A passenger fails to show to the flight before the gate is closed unless delay is due to connecting flight being delayed where in the entire itinerary is present on one or conjunctive QR document(s).</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>A passenger fails to change/cancel his/her reservation 3 hours prior to departure.</li>
<li><span class="icon-arrow-strong icon-rotate-rtl"></span>Any re-booking made within 3 hours prior to departure or after departure of flight as shown in the e-ticket will be considered as a No-show.</li>
</ul>
<p>For a scenario where in the original reservation is cancelled prior to No-show condition, but the new reservation are made after departure of the flight (as mentioned in e-ticket coupon) QR Reservation and Ticketing Staff may perform a manual transaction&nbsp;to avoid the collection of No-show fee.</p>
<p><b>No-show charge:</b></p>
<p>The charge made by reason of the failure of a passenger to use reserved accommodation, either through failure to arrive at the airport at the time fixed by the carrier, or through arriving improperly documented or otherwise not ready to travel on flight.</p>
<p><b>No-show on online checked-in passengers:</b></p>
<p>For bookings that are created in a non-Amadeus GDS system, a customer after having performed an online check-in may later decide to cancel his/her reservation (s) 3 hours prior to the departure of a flight. Under such a scenario although the agent has cancelled the reservation, the passenger will not be offloaded from a flight and is subsequently termed as a No-show passenger. Travel agents (especially non-1A system users) will be required to contact the nearest QR office or a Contact Centre agent who in turn will liaise with the respective airport personnel to ensure that the passenger (s) is offloaded from Qatar Airways Departure Control System (DCS) and subsequently segments can then be cancelled by the agent within their respective GDS.</p>
<p>Non-compliance to the above requirement will result in an ADM being raised.</p>

                    
                    
                </div>
            </div>

		



    </div>

    </div>

   <script>
       $(document).ready(function(){
      var $nodeName = "#table-module-NEHWC-table .C6_1";
      var tableHeaders = [];

      $($nodeName).find('table').removeAttr("cellspacing cellpadding border width");
	  $($nodeName).find('table th').each(function(){
      	tableHeaders.push($(this).text());
      });

	  if ($(window).width() < 767) {
			$($nodeName).find('table tr').each(function(i){
				var $this = $(this);
				$(this).find('td').each(function(index){
					if($(this).attr('rowspan') != undefined){
						$($nodeName).find('table tr').eq(i+1).find('td').eq(index).before('<td>'+$(this).text()+'</td>');
					}
				});
			});
        	$($nodeName).find('th').parent().hide();
      }

	var $tableRows = $($nodeName).find('tr');
      $tableRows.each(function(){
          var t = 0;
          var $tableData = $(this).find('td');
          if($tableData != undefined && $tableData != '') {
      		$tableData.each(function(){
              if(tableHeaders[t] == '&nbsp;'){

              $(this).attr("data-th",'');
              }else {
                $(this).attr("data-th", tableHeaders[t]);
              }
			  if($(window).width() < 767){
					($(this).attr('data-th') != undefined && $(this).attr('data-th').length > 45) ? $(this).css('margin-bottom',($(this).attr('data-th').length/2)+20+'px') : $(this).css('margin-bottom','0');
				}

      		t++;
      
      });
          }

      });
      $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').css('text-align','');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('width');
	  $($nodeName).find('table').find('td').removeAttr('valign');
});
   </script>


      </div>
   


</div>
